    3. There are no major problems with the facilities, but the room I stayed in had continuous noise from unknown equipment at night. The sound was not loud but lasted all night.
    4. The hotel is located in a relatively remote location. Except for a Wanda hotel, the others are newer or under construction. There are construction sites outside the windows. For those who come to Leshan mainly to eat delicious food, it is quite far to go to any famous snack restaurant, making travel quite inconvenient.
    5. One of the two rooms we booked had an obvious sewer smell when we first entered the room.
    The hotel price is not cheap among hotels in Leshan, but overall the experience is very poor. The hotel itself advertises itself as a luxury hotel, but the actual services provided are almost non-existent, even inferior to some ordinary small hotels. This time I am completely disappointed with the Amber brand and will never stay here again.
